Principles Applied\n\n### 1. **Zeigarnik Effect** (Incomplete tasks create tension)\n- Locked steps create curiosity\n- Progress bar shows "almost there"\n- Phases create natural milestones\n- Result: Users want to complete\n\n### 2. **Variable Rewards** (Unpredictable rewards increase engagement)\n- Different guide voices (Merlin vs Rose)\n- Different celebration messages\n- Synchronicities (Step 9) are inherently variable\n- Result: Journey stays interesting\n\n### 3. **Implementation Intentions** (Specific plans increase follow-through)\n- Every step has one clear action\n- Actions are specific ("Say X", "Write 3 names")\n- Checkboxes create commitment\n- Result: Higher completion rates\n\n### 4. **Social Proof** (Others\' behavior influences ours)\n- "X practitioners completed this"\n- Community spotlight examples\n- Shared progress celebrations\n- Result: Feels less solitary, more validated\n\n### 5. **Progress Principle** (Small wins create momentum)\n- Every step completion is celebrated\n- Progress bar fills visually\n- Phase completions are milestones\n- Result: Motivation compounds\n\n### 6. **Autonomy** (Choice increases engagement)\n- Guidance style selector\n- Pace preference\n- Optional features (notes, audio, etc.)\n- Result: Feels personalized, not prescribed\n\n### 7. **Competence** (Mastery feels good)\n- Steps are achievable (2-5 min actions)\n- Clear success criteria (checkboxes)\n- Mastery badge at end (Step 12)\n- Result: Users feel capable\n\n### 8. **Relatedness** (Connection matters)\n- Merlin & Rose as companions\n- Community integration\n- Shared journey with others\n- Result: Users feel supported\n\n---\n\n## Edge Case Scenarios & Solutions\n\n### Scenario 1: User completes journey in 2 days (rushes through)\n**Detection**: Track time between steps\n**Response**: After Step 12, show message:\n- "You completed the journey quickly! For deeper integration, consider revisiting each step over the next 2 weeks and really living the practices."\n**Why**: Honors their pace but encourages depth\n\n### Scenario 2: User stuck on Step 6 for weeks (can\'t anchor code)\n**Detection**: Step 6 active for 14+ days\n**Response**: Show gentle prompt:\n- "Still working on anchoring? That\'s okay. Sometimes this step takes time. Would you like to try the recalibration ritual or ask Merlin & Rose a question?"\n**Why**: Normalizes struggle, offers support\n\n### Scenario 3: User completes Steps 1-5 then disappears for months\n**Detection**: Last active date > 60 days ago\n**Response**: On return, show:\n- "Welcome back! You\'re on Step 6. No pressurepick up when you\'re ready. Your progress is saved."\n**Why**: No shame, easy re-entry\n\n### Scenario 4: User tries to skip to Step 12 (wants shortcut)\n**Detection**: Clicks locked step\n**Response**: Show message:\n- "This step unlocks after completing Step X. Each step builds on the previousskipping weakens the foundation."\n**Why**: Enforces progression, explains why\n\n### Scenario 5: User\'s intention is harmful (to self or others)\n**Detection**: Keyword scan in Step 4 (if implemented)\n**Response**: Show immediate modal:\n- "We notice your intention may involve harm. This system is designed for constructive creation only. If you\'re in crisis, please reach out: [resources]"\n**Why**: Safety boundary, redirects to help\n\n### Scenario 6: User completes journey but sees no results\n**Detection**: User feedback or Step 11 recalibration usage\n**Response**: Step 11 already addresses this, but also:\n- Offer 1-on-1 support (if available)\n- Link to community for peer support\n- Remind: "Sometimes YOU change first, then circumstances"\n**Why**: Realistic expectations, continued support\n\n---\n\n## A/B Testing Opportunities (Future)\n\n### Test 1: Guidance Style Default\n- **A**: Default to "Gentle"\n- **B**: Default to "Practical"\n- **Measure**: Completion rates, user satisfaction\n\n### Test 2: Step Length\n- **A**: Current (3-5 paragraphs teaching)\n- **B**: Shorter (2-3 paragraphs teaching)\n- **Measure**: Drop-off rates, time per step\n\n### Test 3: Action Complexity\n- **A**: Current (simple actions)\n- **B**: Slightly more complex (2-step actions)\n- **Measure**: Completion rates, user feedback\n\n### Test 4: Celebration Frequency\n- **A**: Celebrate every step\n- **B**: Celebrate only phases\n- **Measure**: Motivation, completion rates\n\n### Test 5: Progress Bar Position\n- **A**: Top of page (sticky)\n- **B**: Sidebar (always visible)\n- **Measure**: Engagement, completion rates\n\n---\n\n## Documentation for Your Agent\n\n### File
